        <tr id="so9" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>Reynolds is a light hitting backup middle infielder who got off to a difficult start to his major league career. He recorded an astonishingly high 35% strikeout rate in his 96 plate appearances, after posting a 21% strikeout rate in AAA. However, his 11.9% SwStrk% suggests his K% will drop closer to 22% in the long run. Reynolds also posted a pretty high 54% GB%, which definitely does not bode well when combined with these strikeouts. His position in the Mets system is a bit up in the air at the moment, as he appears to be behind Jose Reyes, Wilmer Flores, and T.J. Rivera in the depth chart. He also may have slipped behind Ty Kelly. All of this considered, it is difficult to imagine Reynolds having any fantasy value in 2017. (Andrew Perpetua)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Reynolds is buried so deep in the depth chart that he may not be able to get plate appearances in 2017, let alone accrue fantasy value.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
